  <script defer="" type="text/javascript">
   var recaptchaOnloadCallback = function () {
            if ($("#recaptcha_div").length) {
                var mainRecaptcha = grecaptcha.render('recaptcha_div', {
                    'sitekey': '6LepVBMTAAAAAFtsPYeaiBKBa5ssaUt2ravj8LwJ',
                    'callback': recaptchaRequiredErase
                });
                $("#recaptcha_div").attr("data-id", mainRecaptcha);
            }
            if ($("#recaptcha_div_share").length) {
                var sharingRecaptcha = grecaptcha.render('recaptcha_div_share', {
                    'sitekey': '6LepVBMTAAAAAFtsPYeaiBKBa5ssaUt2ravj8LwJ',
                    'callback': recaptchaRequiredEraseSharing
                });
                $("#recaptcha_div_share").attr('data-id', sharingRecaptcha);
            }

            //login recaptcha related code
            $("input[data-recaptcha=active]").on('input', function (e) {
                loginInputHandling();
            });
        };

        var loginInputHandling = function () {
            if ($("input[data-recaptcha=active]").length) {
                var allFilledOut = true;
                $("input[data-recaptcha=active]").each(function (index) {
                    if ($(this).val().length === 0) {
                        allFilledOut = false;
                    }
                });

                if (allFilledOut) {
                    $("#submit-button").removeAttr('disabled');
                    $("#submit-button").removeClass('disabled');
                }
            }
        };

        var recaptchaRequiredErase = function () {
            $("#recaptcha_required_input").val("done");
            var input = $("#recaptcha_required_input").validator({
                message: '<div><em/></div>'
            });
            input.data("validator").checkValidity();
            loginInputHandling();
        };

        var recaptchaRequiredEraseSharing = function () {
            $(".js-recaptcha-required-input").val("done");
            var input = $(".js-recaptcha-required-input").validator({
                message: '<div><em/></div>'
            });
            input.data("validator").checkValidity();
        };

        $(document).ready(function () {
            $(".js-captcha-form").submit(function (event) {
                if ($("#recaptcha_required_input").length > 0) {
                    $("#recaptcha_required_input").val(grecaptcha.getResponse($("#recaptcha_div").attr("data-id")));
                    var input = $("#recaptcha_required_input").validator({
                        message: '<div><em/></div>'
                    });
                    input.data("validator").checkValidity();
                }
            });
        });
  </script>
